var shouldShowBanner = false;
if(document.cookie.indexOf('OptanonAlertBoxClosed') === -1){
  shouldShowBanner = true;
} else {
  var cookieString = document.cookie;
  var i = document.cookie.indexOf('OptanonAlertBoxClosed') + ('OptanonAlertBoxClosed=').length;
  var dateString = '';

  while(cookieString[i] && cookieString[i] !== ';') {
    dateString += cookieString[i];
    i++;
  }

  // check if reconsent needed because of onetrust list update
  if(new Date('2022/06/14, 16:51') > new Date(dateString)) {
    shouldShowBanner = true;
  }
}

// user accepted cookie but left the page before onetrust was called
try {
  if(localStorage.getItem('CustomCookieBannerAcceptIntent')) {
    shouldShowBanner = false;
  }
} catch (err) {
  console.warn('Localstorage was not accessible');
}


if(shouldShowBanner) {
  document.documentElement.classList.add('show-cookie-banner');
}
</script><script>
function setGlobalAttributionId() {
  const attributionIdFromQueryString = new URLSearchParams(
    window.location.search
  ).get('tid');

  const attributionIdFromState = window.history.state?.tid
  
  const referrer = document.referrer

  if (attributionIdFromState) {
    window.tid = attributionIdFromState;
  } else if (
    attributionIdFromQueryString &&
    (referrer.includes("typeform.com") ||
      referrer.includes("localhost"))
  ) {
    window.tid = attributionIdFromQueryString;
  }

  if (attributionIdFromQueryString) {
    const urlObj = new URL(window.location.href);
    urlObj.searchParams.delete('tid');

    const urlWithoutAttributionId = urlObj.toString();

    window.history.replaceState(
      {
        ...window.history.state,
        tid: window.tid,
      },
      "",
      urlWithoutAttributionId
    );
  }
}

setGlobalAttributionId();

Please accept or manage your cookie settings below. Here&#x27;s our<!-- --> <a href="https://admin.typeform.com/to/dwk6gt/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">cookie policy</a></p></div><div class="cookie-buttons"><button class="cookie-accept-btn">Accept all cookies</button><button class="cookie-settings-link">Cookie settings</button></div></div><div data-testid="cookie-consent-banner-boundaries" class="cookie-consent-banner-boundaries"></div></div></div><script>
  var settingsClicked = false;
  var isFirstCallbackCall = true;
  var oneTrustCookiesRejectedEvent = new Event('oneTrustCookiesRejected');

  var callSdk = function(callback) {
    if (!document.querySelector('#onetrust-consent-sdk')) {
      setTimeout(function() {
        callSdk(callback)
      }, 100)
    } else {
      callback()
    }
  }

  function hideBanner() {
    var shownBanner = document.querySelector('.show-cookie-banner');

    if(shownBanner) {
      shownBanner.classList.remove('show-cookie-banner')
    }
  }

  function onRejectAllCookies() {
    window.dispatchEvent(oneTrustCookiesRejectedEvent)
  }

  function onShowSettings() {
    settingsClicked = true;

    callSdk(function sdkSettingsCallback() {
      window.OneTrust.ToggleInfoDisplay()

      var rejectAllButton = document.querySelector('.ot-pc-refuse-all-handler');

      if (rejectAllButton) {
        rejectAllButton.addEventListener('click', onRejectAllCookies)
      }

      settingsClicked = false;
    })
  }

  function onAllowAllCookies() {
    try {
      localStorage.setItem('CustomCookieBannerAcceptIntent', true)
    } catch(err) {
      console.warn('Localstorage is not accessible');
    }

    hideBanner();

    callSdk(function sdkAllowCallback() {
      window.OneTrust.AllowAll();
      window.OneTrust.TriggerGoogleAnalyticsEvent('Inhouse Cookie Consent', 'Banner Accept Cookies');

      try {
        localStorage.removeItem('CustomCookieBannerAcceptIntent')
      } catch(err) {
        console.warn('Localstorage is not accessible');
      }
    });
  }

  window.OptanonWrapper = function OptanonWrapper() {
    if (isFirstCallbackCall) {
      isFirstCallbackCall = false;
      return;
    }

    if (!settingsClicked) {
      hideBanner();
    }
  }

  function attachCookieConsentListeners() {
    document.querySelector('.cookie-settings-link').addEventListener('click', onShowSettings);
    document.querySelector('.cookie-accept-btn').addEventListener('click', onAllowAllCookies);
  }

  try {
    if(localStorage.getItem('CustomCookieBannerAcceptIntent')) {
      onAllowAllCookies();
    }
  } catch(err) {
    console.warn('Localstorage is not accessible');
  }

  callSdk(function setLanguage() {
    window?.OneTrust?.changeLanguage?.('en')
  })
  attachCookieConsentListeners();
</script><div class="sc-a494c832-1 bFEFbK"><div class="sc-8dfa07e7-2 kJIglB"><div class="sc-8dfa07e7-0 sc-59615a75-0 brJfVH"><div class="sc-59615a75-1 dDIDtm"><p class="sc-59615a75-2 bJUPEV">Ready to
